<script type="x-jquery-tmpl" id="selectedItemTemplate">
    <div class="clearfix leaderboard-banner-item">
        <div class="dropdown">
            {{if items && items.length > 0}}
                <a href="javascript:;" class="dropdown-toggle" data-toggle="dropdown">
                    <span class="tournament-ellipsis">{{= data.tourName}}</span>
                    <i class="icon-chevron-down"></i>
                </a>
            {{else}}
                <span class="dropdown-toggle tournament-ellipsis">{{= data.tourName}}</span>
            {{/if}}

            <ul class="dropdown-menu">
                {{each(i, item) items}}
                    {{if item.tourName && item.title}}
                        <li>
                            <a href="javascript:;" class="tour-selector" lb-banner-index="{{= item.id}}">
                                {{= item.tourName}} - {{= formatString(item.title, 20, 16)}}
                            </a>
                        </li>
                    {{/if}}
                {{/each}}
            </ul>
        </div>

        {{if data.type == 'weather' || data.type == 'lbMessage'}}
            <span class="tournament-state tournament-ellipsis delayed">
                {{if data.labelOverride && data.labelOverride.length}}
                    {{= data.labelOverride}}
                {{else}}
                    DELAYED
                {{/if}}
            </span>
        {{else data.type == 'standings'}}
            <a href="{{= safeLink(data.standingsPage)}}" class="tournament-state tournament-ellipsis standings">
                {{if data.labelOverride && data.labelOverride.length}}
                    {{= data.labelOverride}}
                {{else}}
                    STANDINGS
                {{/if}}
            </a>
        {{else data.itemData.roundState == 'Groupings Official'}}
            <a href="{{= safeLink(data.teeTimesPage)}}" class="tournament-state tournament-ellipsis tee-times">
                {{if data.labelOverride && data.labelOverride.length}}
                    {{= data.labelOverride}}
                {{else}}
                    TEE TIMES
                {{/if}}
            </a>
        {{else data.itemData.roundState == 'In Progress' || data.itemData.roundState == 'In-Progress'}}
            <a href="{{= safeLink(data.leaderboardPage)}}" class="tournament-state tournament-ellipsis live-now">
                {{if data.labelOverride && data.labelOverride.length}}
                    {{= data.labelOverride}}
                {{else}}
                    LIVE NOW
                {{/if}}
            </a>
        {{else}}
            <a href="{{= safeLink(data.leaderboardPage)}}" class="tournament-state tournament-ellipsis leaderboard">
                {{if data.labelOverride && data.labelOverride.length}}
                    {{= data.labelOverride}}
                {{else}}
                    LEADERBOARD
                {{/if}}
            </a>
        {{/if}}
    </div>

    <p class="title">
        {{if data && data.title}}
            <a href="{{if data.type == 'standings'}}{{= safeLink(data.standingsPage)}}{{else}}{{= safeLink(data.tournamentPage)}}{{/if}}">
                {{= formatString(data.title, 40, 36)}}
            </a>
        {{/if}}
    </p>

</script>

            {{/if}}

    </div>

</script>

<script type="x-jquery-tmpl" id="rcupMatchScoringTemplate">

            <div class="player-cell">
                <a href="{{= getRedirectLink(data)}}">

                    <!-- Left Player -->
                    <span class="left-player-container">
                    {{if match.players[0].matchPlayers.length === 2 }}
                        <span class="player-name player-one">{{= data.itemData.getTeamMember(match.players[0], 0) }}</span>
                        <span class="player-name player-two">{{= data.itemData.getTeamMember(match.players[0], 1) }}</span>
                    {{else}}
                        <span class="player-name left-player">{{= data.itemData.getPlayerName(match.players[0]) }}</span>
                    {{/if}}
                    </span>

                    <!-- Score Information -->
                    <span class="score-container">
                        {{if data.itemData.isPlayerWinner(match.players[0])}}
                            <span class="icon-flag winner"></span>
                        {{else data.itemData.isPlayerLeader(match.players[0])}}
                            <span class="icon-flag leader-left"></span>
                        {{/if}}
                        <span class="player-score bordered">
                            {{html data.itemData.getMatchResult(match, localization.results)}}
                        </span>

                        {{if data.itemData.isPlayerWinner(match.players[1])}}
                            <span class="icon-flag winner-right"></span>
                        {{else data.itemData.isPlayerLeader(match.players[1])}}
                            <span class="icon-flag leader"></span>
                        {{/if}}
                    </span>

                    <!-- Right Player -->
                    <span class="right-player-container">
                    {{if match.players[1].matchPlayers.length === 2 }}
                        <span class="player-name player-one">{{= data.itemData.getTeamMember(match.players[1], 0) }}</span>
                        <span class="player-name player-two">{{= data.itemData.getTeamMember(match.players[1], 1) }}</span>
                    {{else}}
                        <span class="player-name right-player">{{= data.itemData.getPlayerName(match.players[1]) }}</span>
                    {{/if}}
                    </span>
                </a>
            </div>
        {{/each}}
        <div class="player-cell last-fake"></div>
    </div>

</script>

<script type="x-jquery-tmpl" id="matchplayTemplate">
    <div class="item-content players-table match-play">
        {{each(m, match) data.itemData.matches}}
        {{if m < 50}}
        <div class="player-cell">
            <a href="{{= getRedirectLink(data)}}">
                <span class="player-name left-player">{{= match.players[0].displayName}}</span>
                {{if match.players[0].matchWinner.toLowerCase() == 'yes'}}
                    <span class="icon-flag winner"></span>
                {{else match.players[0].matchLeader.toLowerCase() == 'yes'}}
                    <span class="icon-flag leader-left"></span>
                {{else match.players[1].matchLeader.toLowerCase() == 'yes' || match.players[1].matchWinner.toLowerCase() == 'yes'}}
                    <span class="icon-flag empty-left"></span>
                {{/if}}

                <span class="player-score bordered">
                    {{if match.players[0].matchWinner.toLowerCase() == 'yes'}}
                        {{= data.itemData.formatMPScore(match.players[0].finalMatchScr)}}
                    {{else match.players[1].matchWinner.toLowerCase() == 'yes'}}
                        {{= data.itemData.formatMPScore(match.players[1].finalMatchScr)}}
                    {{else match.players[0].matchLeader.toLowerCase() == 'yes'}}
                        {{= data.itemData.formatMPScore(match.players[0].curMatchScr)}} THRU {{= match.players[0].thru}}
                    {{else match.players[1].matchLeader.toLowerCase() == 'yes'}}
                        {{= data.itemData.formatMPScore(match.players[1].curMatchScr)}} THRU {{= match.players[1].thru}}
                    {{else match.players[0].curMatchScr && match.players[0].thru}}
                        {{if match.players[0].thru.toLowerCase() == 'f'}}
                            halved
                        {{else}}
                            AS THRU {{= match.players[0].thru}}
                        {{/if}}
                    {{else}}
                         {{= data.itemData.formatMPTTime(match.players[0].tTime)}}
                    {{/if}}
                </span>

                {{if match.players[1].matchWinner.toLowerCase() == 'yes'}}
                    <span class="icon-flag winner-right"></span>
                {{else match.players[1].matchLeader.toLowerCase() == 'yes'}}
                    <span class="icon-flag leader"></span>
                {{else match.players[0].matchLeader.toLowerCase() == 'yes' || match.players[0].matchWinner.toLowerCase() == 'yes'}}
                    <span class="icon-flag empty-right"></span>
                {{/if}}
                <span class="player-name right-player">{{= match.players[1].displayName}}</span>
            </a>
        </div>
        {{/if}}
        {{/each}}
        <div class="player-cell last-fake"></div>
    </div>

</script>

<script type="text/javascript">
        pgatour.ReactModulesUtils.render(document.querySelector('[data-react-module-name=LeaderboardBanner]'), function () {
            new pgatour.LeaderboardBanner({
                mainContainer: '#leaderboardBannerContainer',
                translationsUrl: '',
                refreshRate: '30',
                contentContainer: '#itemContent',
                sponsorsContainer: '#itemContent .players-table',
                advertisementItem: '#lbAdvertisementItem',
                playersDataContainer: '.leaderboard-banner .players-data',
                dropDownSelector: '.dropdown li a',
                mobileLinkContainer: '#mobileLink',
                mobileLinkTemplate: '#mobileLinkTemplate',
                safeZone: '.leaderboard-banner',
                selectedItemTemplate: '#selectedItemTemplate',
                tournamentDataItem: '.tournament-data',

                presentedByAdContainer: '#presentedByAd',
                scoringByAdContainer: '#scoringByAd',
                rightSideAdContainer: '#rightSideAd',

                itemContentSelector: '.item-content',
                sliderClass: 'player-cell',
                sliderWrapperClass: 'players-table',
                liveTournamentClass: 'live-tournament',
                tournamentDataClass: 'tournament-data',

                teeTimesAdPos: 'tickerspon',
                regularAdPos: 'tickerspon',
                scoringByAdPos: 'tickerleft',
                presentedByAdPos: 'tickerright',

                marketingUnits: 'true',
